A comparison of the old frame macro vs. the new framer macro.
These test indicate frame operation and timing so the new set
can be verified.  As well as space savings from compiling
each section of frame code - per monster or player.

All compilation was done with "fteqcc -Wno-mundane"

//******************************************************
